Macro used internally that can be used externally to make containers easylogging++ friendly. 

@detail This macro expands to write an ostream\& operator\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} for container. This container is expected to have begin() and end() methods that return respective iterators 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Container\+Type} & Type of container e.\+g, My\+List from WX\+\_\+\+DECLARE\+\_\+\+LIST(int, My\+List); in wxwidgets \\
\hline
{\em Size\+Method} & Method used to get size of container. \\
\hline
{\em Element\+Instance} & Instance of element to be fed out. Instance name is "{}elem"{}. See WXELPP\+\_\+\+ENABLED macro for an example usage \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{easylogging_09_09_8h_a5dcfce39a374c368c08aa7c2e95d76f5}\label{easylogging_09_09_8h_a5dcfce39a374c368c08aa7c2e95d76f5}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TIMED\_FUNC\_IF}{TIMED\_FUNC\_IF}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define TIMED\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+IF(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{obj,  }\item[{}]{condition }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~\mbox{\hyperlink{easylogging_09_09_8h_a54df686ae242849f40005c81cd344949}{TIMED\+\_\+\+SCOPE\+\_\+\+IF}}(obj, \mbox{\hyperlink{easylogging_09_09_8h_a918f46ccf9660edaf7797143c489a566}{ELPP\+\_\+\+FUNC}}, condition)}



Performance tracked function. Performance gets written when goes out of scope using \textquotesingle{}performance\textquotesingle{} logger. 

@detail Please note in order to check the performance at a certain time you can use obj-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}checkpoint(); \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
